Banxia Pill

Take two jin of Banxia, peel it, and wash it in river water six or seven times. Take one jin of alum and grind it into powder. Additionally, use four liang each of clove, licorice, grass cardamom, and Shengma, and six liang of sand. Combine these seven ingredients with one dou of good wine and mix them well with Banxia. Soak this mixture, sealing it tightly; for spring and winter, soak for thirty-seven days, and for summer and autumn, soak for seven days. Afterward, take it out daily, wash it quickly in cold water, and let it dry in the wind. Each dose consists of one grain, chewed and swallowed with ginger soup, or taken dry. Wait sixty days before consuming.

Eight-Ingredient Ginger Decoction

For treating minor cough in children, take seven liang of fresh ginger, four liang of dried ginger, two liang of cinnamon bark, three liang each of licorice, coltsfoot flowers, and purple aster, one sheng of apricot kernels, and one sheng of honey. Grind these herbs into a fine powder and decoct them over low heat until they reach a syrupy consistency. Depending on the child's size, provide them a portion to suck and swallow. For infants around a hundred days old, about the size of a jujube pit is appropriate, to be administered four to five times daily, which has proven effective.

Four-Ingredient Pill

For treating a child’s cough that worsens at night, where they initially cannot rest or cry again, take one liang and five qian each of coltsfoot flowers and purple aster, six zhu of Bupleurum root, and half a liang of cinnamon bark. Grind these into powder, mix with honey to form a paste about the size of a jujube pit, and apply it to the nipple for the child to drink from. Administer three times a day, and gradually allow the child to consume it.[37p]

　　菖蒲圆　治小儿暴冷嗽，及积风冷嗽，兼气逆鸣。　　石菖浦　乌头　杏仁　白矾石　北细辛　猪牙皂各六铢　款冬花　干生姜　桂心　紫菀各十八铢　蜀椒五铢　吴茱萸六合　　右十二味为末，蜜丸如梧子。三岁儿饮服五丸，加至十丸，日三。儿小，以意减之；儿大，以意加之。暴嗽，数服便瘥。
　　桂枝汤　治少小十日以上至五十日，卒得謦咳，吐乳呕逆，暴嗽，昼夜不得息。　　桂枝半两　甘草二两五钱　紫菀十八铢　麦门冬一两十八铢　　右四味(口父)咀，以水二升，煮取半升，以绵着汤中，捉绵滴儿口中，昼夜四五过与之，节乳哺。
　　麻黄汤　治少小卒肩息，上气不得安，此恶风入肺。　　麻黄四两　甘草一两　桂心五寸　半夏　生姜各二两　五味子半升　　右六味(口父)咀，以水五升，煮取二升，百日儿服一台，大小节度，服之便愈。[38p]

Aconitum for Treating Children's Sudden Cold Cough: For treating children's sudden cold cough, accumulated wind-cold cough, and reversed Qi causing sound.

  • Ingredients: Six zhù of Stone Aconite, Aconitum, Apricot Kernels, Alumen, North Xi Xin, Pig Tooth Soap; eighteen zhù each of Coltfoot, Dried Ginger, Cinnamon Heart, Purple Aster; five zhù of Sichuan Pepper; six zhù of Wu Zhu Yu.
  • Method: Grind these twelve ingredients into powder, form into pills the size of a walnut. Children aged three can take five pills, with a maximum of ten, three times a day. Adjust the dosage according to the child's size; lesser for smaller children and greater for older ones. For sudden cough, repeated doses lead to quick recovery.

Cinnamon Twig Decoction: Treats children aged ten days to fifty days who suddenly develop a severe cough, vomiting milk, and unable to rest day or night.

  • Ingredients: Half tael of Cinnamon Twigs, two taels and five qian of Licorice, eighteen zhù of Purple Aster, one tael and eighteen zhù of Ophiopogon.
  • Method: Grind these four ingredients, boil with two sheng of water until half a sheng remains. Soak cotton in the decoction and let the child suck it into their mouth, repeating four or five times day and night, adjusting for breastfeeding.

Ephedra Decoction: For treating children with sudden shoulder breath, where the Qi cannot settle due to evil wind entering the lungs.

  • Ingredients: Four taels of Ephedra, one tael of Licorice, five inches of Cinnamon Heart, two taels each of Pinellia and Ginger, half sheng of Schisandra.
  • Method: Grind these six ingredients, boil with five sheng of water until two sheng are left. A hundred-day-old child can take a portion, adjusting for size, and recovery is expected with this treatment.[38p]

　　泻白散 【《钱氏直诀》，下同】 　治肺经实热，咳嗽痰喘。　　桑根白皮炒，泻肺气之有余，有余者，邪有余也　地骨皮各一两　炙甘草五钱　　右为末，每服一二钱，入粳米百粒，水煎。薛己曰：按《活人方》云：喘者，肺气有余也。气盛当认作气衰，有余当认作不足。肺气盛者，乃肺中之火盛也。有余者，肺中之邪有余也。故用前药以泻之。若土虚不能生肺，用补中益气汤；火来克金，用人参平肺散；肾水夺母之气，或阴火上炎，用地黄丸。若肺虚肝木乘悔，先用阿胶散，后用泻青丸。若因乳母肺经受证，致儿为患，母服前散。若因乳母感冒风寒，肺经郁热，致儿为患，用十味参苏饮。若因乳母膏粱醇酒积热，致儿为患，用加味清胃散。
　　泻黄散　治脾胃气热，大肠不利，致令肺病。　　藿香　甘草各七钱五分　山栀仁炒，一两　石膏五钱　防风二两　　右，蜜酒微炒为末，水煎服。[39p]

Xie Bai San (Dissolving White Powder)
Treats excess heat in the lung channel, cough with phlegm and wheezing.
Fried mulberry root white skin, used to drain excess lung qi; excess indicates lingering pathogens.
Ground together: di guo peel, 1 tael; honey-fried licorice, 5 qian.
Grind these into a powder, and for each dose, take 1-2 qian mixed with 100 grains of polished rice, then boil in water. Xue Ji said: According to the "Living Person's Prescriptions", wheezing indicates excess lung qi. When qi is vigorous, it should be understood as deficient, and when excess is present, it should be regarded as insufficient. Excess lung qi is actually the fire within the lungs being high. Therefore, the previous herbs are used to drain it. If the earth is deficient and cannot generate the lungs, use Bu Zhong Yi Qi Decoction; if the fire is attacking metal, use Ren Shen Ping Fei San; if kidney water is taking away the mother’s qi or the yin fire is flaming upwards, use Di Huang Wan. If lung deficiency causes the liver wood to overpower, first use Ejiao San and afterwards use Xie Qing Wan. If due to the nursing mother's lung channel being afflicted, causing issues for the child, the mother should take the above powder. If the nursing mother catches wind and cold, with lung channel heat, leading to issues for the child, use Shi Wei Shen Su Yin. If it is due to the nursing mother’s consumption of rich and warm foods, causing heat accumulation and affecting the child, use Jia Wei Qing Wei San.

Xie Huang San (Dissolving Yellow Powder)
Treats heat of the spleen and stomach qi, leading to difficulty in the large intestine, which can result in lung disease.
Ingredients: Huo Xiang and licorice, each 7.5 qian; fried gardenia fruit, 1 tael; gypsum, 5 qian; Fang Feng, 2 taels.
Grind these together, slightly fry with honey and wine, then take as a decoction.[39p]

　　地黄丸　治心火炎烁肺经，致令肺病。　　熟地黄八钱，杵膏　山茱萸肉　干山药各四钱　泽泻　牡丹皮　白茯苓各三钱　　右为末，用地黄膏量加米糊，丸桐子大，空心白汤化下。其地黄用生者，自制杵膏。
　　阿胶散　治肺虚肺疳，咳嗽痰吐稠粘，口干作渴。《幼科全书》云：此补肺之药。　　明阿胶一两，麸炒能补气不足　炙甘草一钱　马兜铃五钱，主肺热咳嗽，清肺补肺　糯米一两　杏仁七个，去皮尖，下喘治气　鼠粘子二钱五分　　右为末，每服二钱。薛己曰：按前证，若因脾胃弱而肺气虚者，宜用补中益气汤；若肺金自虚者，宜用四君子汤。
　　百部丸　治肺寒壅嗽微喘。
　　杏仁去皮尖，四十个，微炒水煮三五沸　百部炒　麻黄去节，各三钱　　右研如泥，用炼蜜丸皂子大，每服一二丸，姜汤化下。一方加松子仁五十个，蜜丸，更加胡桃含化大妙。一方加甘草二钱。[40p]

Di Huang Wan: Treats the fiery inflammation of the heart affecting the lung channels, causing lung disease. Use eight qian of cooked Rehmannia, four qian each of Chuanxiong fruit, dried Chinese yam, three qian each of Alisma, tree peony bark, and white poria. Grind these into a powder, then use Rehmannia paste, adding in rice paste, to form pills the size of a tung seed. Consume them in warm water. Use fresh Rehmannia to prepare the paste.

E Jiao San: Treats lung deficiency and lung sores, with symptoms of coughing up thick and sticky phlegm, dry mouth, and thirst. The "Complete Book of Pediatrics" states this is a remedy for lung reinforcement. Use one liang of E Jiao (donkey-hide gelatin), properly roasted wheat bran to replenish insufficient qi, one qian of roasted licorice root, five qian of Aristolochia, which is suitable for lung heat cough to clear and nourish the lungs, one liang of glutinous rice, seven peeled apricot kernels for easing asthma, and two and a half qian of mouse sticky seeds. Grind these into a powder and take two qian at a time. Xue Ji advises that if caused by a weak spleen and stomach leading to lung qi deficiency, Reinforcing the Middle and Benefiting Qi Decoction is appropriate. If the lung metal is deficient, use the Four Gentlemen Decoction.

Bai Bu Wan: Treats lung cold causing cough and slight wheezing. Use forty peeled apricot kernels, lightly roasted and boiled for three to five minutes, three qian each of roasted Bai Bu and Ma Huang without joints. Grind these into a paste and mix with honey to form pills the size of soapberries. Consume one or two pills with ginger soup. One variation adds fifty pine nuts, mixing with honey to form pills and enhances effectiveness with walnuts for oral dissolution. Another variation adds two qian of licorice root.[40p]

　　麻黄汤　治伤风发热无汗，咳嗽喘急。　　麻黄去节，三钱，水煮去沫，漉出晒干　肉桂二钱　炙甘草一钱　杏仁七个，去皮尖，麸炒黄研膏　每服一钱，水煎服，以汗出为度。自汗者不宜服。薛己曰：按前方，乃发表出汗之剂，审其寒邪在表，宜用。若邪既去，宜补脾肺以实其表，庶风邪不能再入。往往表散之后，热嗽不退，复行发表，多变坏证。
　　葶苈丸　治伤风咳嗽，面亦身热，痰盛喘促。　　甜葶苈隔纸略炒　黑牵牛炒　杏仁炒黄研膏　汉防己各一两　　右为末，入杏膏蒸枣肉捣丸麻子大，每服十丸，姜汤下。薛己曰：按前方行气导湿之峻剂。若脾肺虚热而致诸证者，当调补中气为主。若果系前证，宜用惺惺散、参苏饮、清肺丸、茯苓半夏汤选用之。
　　惺惺散　治伤寒时气，风热痰壅咳嗽。　　桔梗　细辛　人参　炙草　白伏苓　白朮炒　瓜蒌根各等分　　右为末，每服二钱，入薄荷五叶水煎。[41p]

Ma Huang Decoction: Treats common cold with fever and no sweat, cough, and wheezing.
Ma Huang (dried, without the branches), 9 grams, boil in water to remove the foam, strain and dry.
Cinnamon, 6 grams
Honey-fried Licorice, 3 grams
Almonds, 7 pieces, skin and tip removed, fried with bran until yellow and ground into paste.
Take 3 grams each dose, decoct in water; adjust dosage based on sweating. Those who sweat easily should not take it. Xue Ji said: This formula is for dispersing and inducing sweating; examine if the cold pathogen is affecting the surface, then it is appropriate to use it. If the pathogen is already dispelled, one should tonify the spleen and lungs to fortify the surface, so that wind pathogens cannot re-enter. Often, after dispersing the surface, if the heat cough does not subside, repeated attempts to induce sweat may lead to adverse conditions.

Ting Li Pill: Treats common cold with cough, also heat in the face and body, excessive phlegm, and shortness of breath.
Sweet Ting Li, slightly stir-fried with paper;
Black Cowherb, stir-fried;
Almonds, stir-fried and ground;
Han Fángjǐ, each 30 grams.
The above should be made into a powder, mixed with almond paste and steamed jujube flesh, formed into pills the size of sesame seeds. Each dose is 10 pills, taken with ginger decoction. Xue Ji said: This formula is a potent remedy for promoting qi and draining dampness. If symptoms are caused by deficiency heat of the spleen and lungs, the main strategy should focus on tonifying central qi. If indeed it corresponds to previous symptoms, it is advisable to select from formulas like Xingxing San, Shen Su Decoction, Qing Fei Wan, and Fu Ling Ban Xia Decoction.

Xing Xing San: Treats febrile diseases due to wind-heat with phlegm blockage and cough.
Platycodon, Xixin, Ginseng, Honey-fried Licorice, White Poria, Stir-fried Atractylodes, and Gourd Root, each in equal parts.
Make a powder; each dose is 6 grams, decoct in water with 5 leaves of mint.[41p]

　　参苏饮　治感冒风寒，或腹胀少食，泄泻呕吐，或手足并冷，喘促痰涎。　　人参　紫苏　陈皮　前胡　半夏　茯苓　枳壳麸炒　桔梗炒　干葛　甘草炒，各五分　木香三分　　右为末，每服一二钱，姜枣水煎服。
　　茯苓半夏汤　治胃气虚弱，痰涎恶心，或饮食不化，呕吐发搐，或睡卧不宁，口流痰涎；乳母脾胃虚弱，饮食不节，以致儿患前证，亦宜用此药主之。　　白朮土炒　茯苓　半夏　神曲炒，各一钱　大麦炒，五钱　陈皮　天麻各三钱　　右，每服一二钱，水煎。

　　甘桔散　治咳吐热涎，咽喉不利，小儿肺热，手掐眉目鼻面。　　甘草炒，二两　桔梗一两，米泔浸焙　　右为末，每服二钱，入炮阿胶半片，水煎服。薛己曰：按前证若风热蕴于肺而咳脓血，用桔梗汤；若心克于肺而吐痰涎，用人参平肺散。[42p]

Ginseng and Perilla Drink: Used to treat colds caused by wind and cold, or symptoms such as abdominal distension, reduced appetite, diarrhea, vomiting, cold hands and feet, wheezing, and phlegm. Ingredients: Ginseng, perilla, aged tangerine peel, front-hu, pinellia, poria, stir-fried bitter orange peel, stir-fried platycodon, dried kudzu, stir-fried licorice, each five parts; musk three parts. Grind these together into a powder, and take one or two qian (a unit of weight) each time, decocted with ginger and jujube water.

Poria and Pinellia Decoction: Used to treat weak stomach qi, phlegm and nausea, undigested food, vomiting and spasms, or restlessness during sleep with saliva flow. For nursing mothers with weak spleen and stomach due to irregular diet, causing similar symptoms in infants, this remedy is also appropriate. Ingredients: Stir-fried atractylodes, poria, pinellia, and fried shenqu, each one qian; roasted barley five qian; tangerine peel and gastrodia three qian each. Grind these together, and take one or two qian each time, decocted in water.

Licorice and Tangerine Powder: Used to treat cough with heat phlegm, difficulty in the throat, and for children with lung heat, along with facial symptoms such as clenched hands and contorted features. Ingredients: Stir-fried licorice, two liang (a larger unit of weight); one liang of platycodon; soaked and roasted rice wash. Grind these into a powder, and take two qian each time with half a piece of fried ejiao, decocted in water. Xue Ji noted that for the previous symptoms if wind-heat is entrenched in the lungs causing purulent blood cough, use platycodon decoction; if the heart affects the lungs causing phlegm, use ginseng lung calming powder.[42p]

　　桔梗汤　治咳嗽吐脓，痰中有血，已成肺痈证。　　桔梗炒　贝每　当归酒浸　薏苡仁　瓜蒌仁　枳壳麸炒　桑白皮炒　百合蒸，各一钱五分　五味子炒　甜葶苈炒　地骨皮　知母炒　甘草节　防己　黄芪炒　杏仁各五分　　右，每服一二钱，水煎。

　　人参平肺散　治心火克肺，咳嗽喘呕，痰涎壅盛，胸膈痞满。　　人参　　橘红　炙甘草　地骨皮各五分　茯苓　知母炒，各七分　五味子炒　青皮　天门冬各四分　桑白皮炒，一钱　　右，每服一二钱，水煎。

　　凉膈丸 【《圣惠方》】 　治小儿热嗽。　　甘草二两，猪胆浸五宿，炙研末
　　右，蜜丸菉豆大，食后，薄荷汤下十丸。
　　夺命散 【《儒门事亲》】 　治小儿胸膈喘满。　　黑牵牛　白牵牛皆当各半，生熟用之　槟榔　大黄各等分　　右为细末，蜜水调服之。[43p]

Jiegeng Decoction: Treats cough with purulent phlegm, blood in phlegm, signs of lung abscess. Ingredients: Jiegeng stir-fried, Beimu, Danggui (soaked in wine), Yiyiren, Guoluren, Zhike fried with bran, Sangbai Pi fried, Baihe steamed, each 1.5 qian; Wuweizi stir-fried, Tianshuicai stir-fried, Digupi, Zhi Mu stir-fried, Gancao jie, Fangji, Huangqi stir-fried, and Xingren, each 0.5 qian. Decoction: Take 1-2 qian each time, boiled with water.

Ren Shen Ping Fei San: Treats heart fire affecting the lungs, cough, asthma, nausea, excessive phlegm, and chest fullness. Ingredients: Ren Shen, Juhong, Zhi Gancao, Digupi, each 0.5 qian; Fuling, Zhimuh, each 0.7 qian; Wuweizi stir-fried, Qingpi, Tianmendong, each 0.4 qian; Sangbai Pi fried, 1 qian. Decoction: Take 1-2 qian each time, boiled with water.

Liang Ge Wan (from "Sheng Hui Fang"): Treats heat cough in children. Ingredients: 2 liang of Gancao, 5 nights of pig bile soaked, stir-fried and ground into powder. Form into honey pills the size of mung beans; take ten pills after meals with mint decoction.

Duo Ming San (from "Ru Men Shi Qing"): Treats chest fullness and asthma in children. Ingredients: Heiqianniu and Baiqianniu, each half, used either raw or cooked; Binglang, Dahuang, each equal portions. Grind into fine powder, mix with honey water for administration.[43p]

　　麻黄定喘汤 【东垣】 　治小儿寒郁而喘，喉鸣，腹内鸣，坚满，鼻流清涕，脉沉急而数。　　麻黄　草豆蔻各一钱　益智仁一分半　厚朴　吴茱萸各二分　甘草　柴胡　生黄芩各一分　归尾　苏木　升麻　神曲各半分　红花少许　全蝎一枚　　右，分二服，水一大盏，煎七分，稍热服，食远。忌风寒，微汗效。
　　五圣丹 【《幼科全书》，下同】
　　南星煨　陈皮盐水炒，各一两　半夏泡，二两　杏仁另研，四十九粒　甘草五钱　先以南星、半夏二味另研，同姜汁，皂角汁拌匀，合作面，取出，再用甘草、陈皮研为细末，别取竹沥一碗，将前末捏成饼子焙干，又浸又焙，沥尽为度，再研入杏泥蒸蜜和丸，临卧噙一丸，薄荷汤咽下。
　　苏沈九宝汤　此发散之轻药也。
　　桑白皮去赤　甘草　大腹皮　官桂　薄荷叶　苏叶　麻黄不去根节　陈皮　杏仁不去皮尖　　右加乌梅、姜一片，煎服微汗。[44p]

Mahuang Dingchuan Decoction
(From Dongyuan)
Treats children's cold obstruction and wheezing, noisy throat, abdominal sounds, fullness, clear nasal discharge, and a pulse that is deep, urgent, and rapid.
Ingredients:

  • Mahuang: 1 qian
  • Caodoukou: 1 qian
  • Yizhiren: 1.5 fen
  • Houpian: 2 fen
  • Wuzhuyu: 2 fen
  • Gancao: 1 fen
  • Chaihu: 1 fen
  • Shenghuangqin: 1 fen
  • Guwei: 0.5 fen
  • Sumu: 0.5 fen
  • Shengma: 0.5 fen
  • Shenqu: 0.5 fen
  • Honghua: a little
  • Quanzhe: 1 piece
    Preparation:
    Divide into two doses, use a large cup of water, boil down to two-thirds, and take warm on an empty stomach. Avoid wind and cold, and sweating should be mild.

Wusheng Dan
(From "Complete Book of Pediatrics")
Ingredients:

  • Nanning: 2 liang, roasted
  • Chenpi: 2 liang, stir-fried in salt water
  • Banxia: 2 liang, soaked
  • Xingren: 49 pieces, ground separately
  • Gancao: 5 qian
    Preparation:
    First, grind Nanning and Banxia separately, mix with ginger juice and soapberry juice. Combine to form a dough, take it out, and separately grind Gancao and Chenpi into a fine powder. Take one bowl of bamboo juice, knead the mixture into small cakes, dry them by baking, and then soak and bake again until done. Finally, mix into apricot paste with honey and form balls. Before sleeping, dissolve one ball in mint tea.

Su Shen Jiubao Decoction
This is a light dispersing medicine.
Ingredients:

  • Sangbaipi (white mulberry bark, excluding red)
  • Gancao
  • Dafu pi (big belly peel)
  • Guangui (cinnamon)
  • Bohe ye (mint leaves)
  • Suye (perilla leaves)
  • Mahuang (not stripped at the root)
  • Chenpi
  • Xingren (apricots, not stripped or pointed)
    Preparation:
    Add Wumei (Chinese plum) and a piece of ginger, boil and consume to induce mild sweating.[44p]

Wuhutang
This is a strong medicinal formula for dispelling.
7 parts Ephedra, 1 penny of Apricot kernels, 4 parts Licorice, 8 parts Fine Tea, 0.5 penny of Gypsum. Boil in water and take to induce sweating, avoiding wind.

Maogen Soup
Dried Tangerine Peel without the white part, 4 parts Pinellia, Poria, Licorice, Asparagus, Scutellaria, Gardenia seeds, Fritillaria, Anemarrhena, Gypsum, Raw Rhubarb, Platycodon, Apricot kernel paste, Trichosanthes powder. Combine with 1 cup of water, mash Maogen to extract its natural juice, mix, and boil for consumption.

Guanju Soup
Platycodon, Licorice, Apricot kernel paste. Boil in water and consume, mixing with half a cup of bamboo sap, swallowing slowly.

Chronic Cough Formula
For treating children with cough due to food stagnation.
4 parts Dried Tangerine Peel, 4 parts Bitter Orange Peel, 3 parts Fermented Pinellia, 3 parts Licorice, 3 parts Platycodon, stir-fried Huanglian, 8 parts Poria, Earth Bone Skin, Ophiopogon, Hawthorn flesh, 6 parts Huangqin, Trichosanthes fruit, 5 parts Anemarrhena, Mulberry bark, Pueraria powder. Prepare and boil with ginger.

Tianma Powder
For treating infantile cough with phlegm, causing reddened face due to chest congestion.
Southern Star (Zhejiang) soaked for 5 days, with half a tael, 3 qian of Tianma, 1 qian of Cinnabar, and a pinch of Musk. Grind all into powder; take a pinch mixed with Apricot kernel soup, Ginseng soup is also acceptable.[45p]

　　琥珀散　治小儿急慢惊风，涎潮昏冒，目瞪搐搦，惊吊肚疼，及和顺痘疮小可，惊哭，眠卧不安。　　辰砂一钱半　琥珀　牛黄　僵蚕炒去丝嘴　全蝎去毒　白附子　乳香另研　蝉蜕去土　代赭石煅酢淬七次　牛胆　南星各一钱　麝香　冰片各一字　　右为细末，每服一钱，薄荷汤下。《证治准绳》有天麻。慢惊加附子。
　　天麻丸　治小儿未满百晬，咳嗽不止，名曰乳嗽。　　川芎一两半　生甘草二两　硼砂半两　天麻　蝉蜕　僵蚕　人参　辰砂　天竺黄　雄黄　白附子　坯各一两　金箔五片　　右为末，炼蜜丸如芡实大，金箔为衣，每服一丸，薄荷汤下。《证治准绳》加牛胆南星。
　　葛根芩连汤　治太阳病反下之，利遂不止，脉促者喘而汗出。　　葛根二两　黄芩　黄连各七钱半　生甘草半两　　右(口父)咀、每服三钱，水一盏，煎七分，去滓加减服。喘甚加葶苈子。[46p]

Amber powder treats children's sudden or chronic convulsions, excessive salivation, confusion, staring and twitching, abdominal pain due to fright, and mild variola with crying and restless sleep.

1.5 taels of cinnabar, amber, cow bile, roasted silkworms with threads removed, scorpions with toxins removed, white atractylodes, frankincense ground separately, cicada molt with soil removed, red ochre calcined and washed seven times, cow gallbladder, and southern star (each 1 tael), along with musk and borneol (each a small quantity).

The above should be finely powdered. Each dose is 1 tael, taken with mint decoction. “Zheng Zhi Zhun Sheng” mentions Tianma. For chronic convulsions, add aconite.

Tianma Pill is for treating children under a hundred days old who cough without cessation, known as infantile cough.

1.5 taels of chuanxiong, 2 taels of fresh licorice, 0.5 taels of borax, Tianma, cicada molt, silkworms, ginseng, cinnabar, zhu jing (golden flower), realgar, white atractylodes, and prepared earth (each 1 tael), along with 5 pieces of gold leaf.

The above should be ground into powder, and made into pills the size of lotus seeds, with the gold leaf as a coating. Each dose is 1 pill, taken with mint decoction. “Zheng Zhi Zhun Sheng” suggests adding cow bile and southern star.

Ge Gen Qin Lian Decoction is for treating Taiyang disease, where purging has been ineffective, with persistent diarrhea, and rapid pulse indicating dyspnea and sweating.

2 taels of kudzu root, 0.75 taels each of scutellaria and coptis, and 0.5 taels of fresh licorice.

The above should be ground (or used as directed), with each dose being 3 taels, mixed with one cup of water, simmered down to 75%, strained, and adjusted for dosage. If suffering severe dyspnea, add the seeds of prunella.[46p]

　　梅花饮子　治婴孩惊热、潮热、虚热、积热、五脏蕴热、上焦壅热、手足心热，喉中多痰，面色或红或白，变蒸嗞呀，鼻流清涕，气急，肝肺壅热，目赤咳嗽；或被人物所惊，使啼睡卧不安，心中惊怖，情绪不快；或伤寒渐安，尚有余热未除，亦宜进此三两服。常服镇心压惊，化痰退热安神，可除未来之患。　　硼砂　马牙硝　芒硝俱另研　甘草炙，各半两　人参一两　辰砂二钱半　片脑　麝香各一字　　右八味为末，以磁器收之，遇有此证，服一匙，麦门冬汤调下。气喘咳嗽，桑白皮汤调下；常服薄荷汤下。
　　吴子玉方　治证同前。
　　白色信石一字，并下豆粉研泡过用　生南星　枯矾各一钱　鹅管石　硼砂各半钱　菉豆粉　雄黄各一钱半　　右为末，糊丸如萝卜子大，临卧用冷茶清吞下五丸。[47p]

Plum Blossom Drink is used to treat infants with symptoms such as fright fever, tidal fever, deficiency heat, accumulated heat, internal heat in the five organs, heat congested in the upper jiao, palms and soles feeling hot, excess phlegm in the throat, flushed or pale complexion, signs of irritability, runny nose, wheezing, liver and lung heat, eye redness and cough; or distress caused by external fright leading to restless crying and sleeping, feelings of fear and emotional discomfort; or residual heat persisting after recovering from an illness, it is advisable to take this remedy in doses of three to two. Regular consumption can calm the heart, alleviate fright, disperse phlegm, reduce heat, and soothe the spirit, which can prevent future ailments.

Ingredients:

  • Borax, horse tooth nitre, and mirabilite, each ground separately, half a tael each.
  • Ginseng, one tael.
  • Realgar, two and a half qian.
  • Nux vomica and musk, each a character (a small quantity).

Mix the above eight ingredients into a fine powder, stored in ceramic ware. For symptoms, take one spoonful, mixed with Ophiopogon decoction. For wheezing and coughing, take it mixed with mulberry bark decoction; regular consumption can be taken with mint tea.

Wu Ziyu's formula is used for the same symptoms.

For the white stone, grind it down with powdered beans to infuse and use.

  • Raw South Star, and burnt alum, each one qian.
  • Goose pipe stone and borax, each half qian.
  • Pea powder and yellow arsenic, each one and a half qian.

Mix to a powder, make into pills about the size of a radish seed, and take five pills with cold tea before bed.[47p]

Banxia Pill: Treats lung Qi disorders, cough, wheezing, fullness, phlegm and saliva stagnation, hardness and fullness in the heart region, shortness of breath, irritability, wind blocking phlegm, dizziness, difficulty in swallowing, vomiting, nausea, confusion of mind, palpitations with face heat, and sticky nasal discharge—all these are treated.

Ingredients:

  • 2.5 taels of dried alum
  • 3 taels of Banxia, washed with water to remove its slickness, soaked in ginger juice overnight.

Grind the above into a fine powder, form into pills the size of a wutong seed using natural ginger juice. Take 10 or 20 pills after meals when lying down with ginger soup. For children, make the pills the size of a sesame seed.

Baoshou Powder:
Ingredients:

  • 1 tael each of white poria, ginseng, Sichuan aconite, and processed gypsum
  • A small quantity of musk and cow bile (optional)
  • Four words of brain powder

Grind these eight ingredients finely, mix them in a tin container, using hot water until they become a fine powder.

Xiao Guiming Powder: Treats children's fever, cold, chills, extreme heat, clear nasal discharge, coughing, overall warmth, and phlegm in the throat, along with previous symptoms of cold; helps to calm febrile conditions, reduce phlegm, and maintain health.

Ingredients:

  • 0.5 tael each of white poria, ginseng, and white atractylodes
  • 3 qian of licorice
  • 2 qian of cinnabar
  • A small amount of brain powder and musk

Grind these seven ingredients into a powder, take 0.5 qian mixed with mint tea as a decoction.[48p]

　　解肌散　治婴孩伤寒伤风，面部红赤嗞呀，浑身壮热，有前项等形证，兼服人参散，后得热退，可观患势轻重，若患稍轻，脉候不洪数，面不大赤，不加烦躁，然须呻吟讝语，此为轻可之候，但只进此。　　人参　钓藤　桔梗　甘草　川芎各三钱　葶苈一钱，炒　白茯苓二钱　杏仁四十九个　石膏煅　麻黄去节，各四两　　右銼散，每服二钱，枣一枚，水一盏，煎半盏服。如初中伤寒，先下此药，是须要仔细辨认形证，若是麻痘疮疹，便不得下此药。盖麻痘之证，则面青白耳珠，脚膝尻骨俱冷如冰，身体温壮，亦狂躁讝语，梦中惊笑，乃是此候也。若小儿伤寒等服此解肌散，渐得热退，次第可服大归命散、保寿散、轻粉白朮散等调理。[49p]

Jiexī Sàn: This formula treats infants with common colds or fevers, characterized by a red, flushed face, fever throughout the body, stiffness in the neck and similar symptoms. When combined with Rénshēn Sàn, the fever may subside later on. The severity of the condition can be observed; if the symptoms are mild, with a pulse that is not rapid or strong, a face that is not overly red, and no increased irritability—just some groaning and murmuring—this indicates a lighter condition, but only this formula should be administered.

Ingredients:

  • Ginseng, vine of Diao (钓藤), Platycodon, licorice, and Chuanxiong, each 3 qian (approximately 9 grams).
  • A 1 qian (around 3 grams) of stir-fried Qingli (葶苈).
  • 2 qian (about 6 grams) of white Poria.
  • 49 pieces of apricot kernel.
  • 4 liang (approximately 150 grams) of gypsum, calcined, and Ephedra (麻黄), with stems removed.

This combination should be ground into a fine powder. Each dose should be 2 qian, with one jujube and a cup of water, boiled down to half a cup to be taken. If the infant suffers from initial febrile illness, this medication should be administered first, ensuring careful recognition of symptoms. If it is measles, this medication should not be used. In cases of measles, the face appears pale and bluish, earlobes, knees, and tailbone feel cold like ice, the body is warm and strong, and signs of excitement and murmuring occur in dreams—these indicate that particular condition.

If a child with fever receives this Jiexī Sàn and gradually recovers, they can subsequently take Dà Guīmìng Sàn, Bǎoshòu Sàn, or Qingfěn Bái Zhú Sàn for further recuperation.[49p]

Baiyu Pill: This treats obstruction of phlegm and saliva in the diaphragm, alleviates persistent chest discomfort, and reduces coughing with excessive phlegm. Ingredients: Nanshing, Banxia, Jiangcan, and Baifan (both raw and cooked), each two and a half qian. Take 10 to 20 pills each time, swallowed with ginger soup, without time restrictions.

Pediatric Cough and Wheezing Method:

Six Gentlemen Decoction: This is for treating qi deficiency of the spleen and stomach that fails to nourish, leading to lung issues. Ingredients: Ginseng, Baizhu, Fuling, Licorice, Chenpi, and Banxia, each in equal quantities. For use, take two qian, decoct in ginger and jujube water.

Daqing Ointment: This treats lung excess combined with wind-cold, causing chest fullness, shortness of breath, and rapid, wheezing cough. Ingredients: Tianma and Qingtai, each one qian; Bai Fu (baked white attached), black snake meat soaked in wine and baked, and scorpion tail, both five fen; Tianzhuhuang and Musk, each one character. Grind into a powder, form into honey pills the size of beans, and take half a pill dissolved in mint soup.

The above text describes various traditional Chinese herbal formulas for specific ailments, along with their preparations and dosages.

  1. For Pain Relief:

    • Boil the ingredients in water for consumption. If ineffective, add 20 grains of salt and fermented soybeans.

  2. Daoshi Powder (for treating heat in the lung channel in children):

    • Ingredients: equal parts Rehmannia Root, Akebia, and Licorice.
    • Grind to a fine powder. Take one qian (approximately 3 grams) each time, add light bamboo leaves, boil in water.

  3. Yihuang Powder (for treating lung channel deficiency with symptoms including wheezing, facial flushing, heat, and phlegm):

    • Ingredients: 1 liang (approximately 30 grams) dried orange peel, 5 qian each of green peel, haritaki pulp, and roasted licorice, and 2 qian of clove.
    • Grind to a fine powder. Take two qian each time, boil in water.

  4. Qianghuo Powder (for tackling liver obstruction affecting the lungs with symptoms like wind sensitivity, dizziness, and confusion):

    • Ingredients: 0.5 liang each of Siler, Ligusticum, Ginseng, White Atractylodes, and red Poria; 1 liang of Gastrodia; and various other ingredients including dried silkworms and white flower snake meat, all in specific measurements.
    • Grind finely, combine with honey to form pills the size of broad beans. Take three pills before meals, either with mint soup or Ophiopogon soup. Caution: Do not take if there is real heat or severe fright, as it is warming in nature.[51p]

Ginseng and Atractylodes Powder
Treats spleen and lung deficiency with phlegm, symptoms include heaviness, vomiting phlegm, diarrhea, and cough.
Ingredients: Ginseng, Atractylodes (stir-fried), Agastache leaves, Costus root, Licorice, White Poria (each one qian), Dried Kudzu (two qian).
Method: Grind finely, add one slice of fresh ginger, one cup of water, boil down to seven parts, strain and take warm, without time restriction.

Four Noble Ginseng Decoction [from "Secret Records"]
Treats weak lung qi in children.
Ingredients: Equal parts of Ginseng, Atractylodes, Poria, Licorice.
Method: Each dose is two qian, boiled in water.

Great Purging Decoction [from "Xue's Medical Cases"]
Treats fullness and distention in the central body of children.
Ingredients: Rhubarb, Glauber's salt (each five qian), Magnolia bark (one tael), processed ginger, stir-fried bitter orange.
Method: Boil in water to take.

Different Effects Powder [from "Qian's Direct Method"]
Treats spleen's inability to nourish the lungs, with reversed qi causing cough, abdominal fullness, facial swelling, and loss of appetite.
Ingredients: Equal parts of Ginseng, Atractylodes, Poria, stir-fried Licorice, stir-fried Tangerine peel.
Method: Grind to a powder, each dose is three qian, boiled with ginger and jujube water.

Lily Decoction [from "Comprehensive Health Essentials"]
Treats wind-cold affecting the lung channels with phlegm obstruction.
Ingredients: One tael each of Lily, Aster (washed and dried), Atractylodes, Ginseng; half a tael each of White Poria, Green tangerine peel, Licorice, and Ophiopogon.
Method: Grind to a powder, each dose is one qian, with eight parts water, three slices of bamboo leaves, two mint leaves, boil down to five parts, strain and take warm, without time restriction.[52p]

To treat lung qi disorders.

Platycodon Decoction (from "Principles of Diagnosis and Treatment"):

To treat children's cough, chest discomfort, and internal heat symptoms with a flushed face after drinking water.

Bian Yin Pill (from "Xue's Medical Cases"):

To treat cough, body heat with sticky phlegm, inability to digest milk and food, abdominal distension, and rough breathing.
Ingredients: bitter bean (removing oily membrane), finely ground frost - half tael; mercury - five qian; lead - two and a half qian; combine with mercury and bake into sand; vinegar roasted and ground - eight qian; musk, ground separately - five fen.
Mix together the bitter bean powder and the sand, along with musk, with aged rice porridge to form pills the size of mung beans. "Group Ginseng Pills" treat coughing blood.

The ingredients include:

  • Ejiao (donkey-hide gelatin)
  • Soapberry (zhào zi) – half a tael each of ginseng
  • Remove the gelatin and grind it into a fine powder. Melt some in water and combine, forming a size of a chickpea, then take with warm water.

"Chicken Clean Powder" (from the Zhu family) treats coughing with blood and excessive salivation.

Ingredients:

  • Half a tael of turmeric
  • One measure of soapberry water, or cook until dry with pickled cabbage juice
  • Half a tael of raw talcum powder
  • Half a tael of orpiment boiled with vinegar until half dry

Grind these into a fine powder. For each dose, take one character (a small measure) with mint tea; for stopping coughs, take with snail powder water; for coughing blood, take with clear chicken broth.

"Add-Flavored Refreshing Powder" (similar to “Zhengzhi Zhunspring”) is used for colds, chills, phlegm coughs, counteracting qi deficiency, calming the mind, clearing the skin, stopping crying and annoyance, benefiting the throat, and relieving loss of voice.

Ingredients:

  • Half a tael of ginseng
  • One tael each of stir-fried balloon flower root, white poria, and stir-fried white atractylodes
  • One tael of tianhua fen (trichosanthes root)
  • Two qian of xi xin (wild ginger)
  • Two and a half qian each of fang feng (siler) and chuān xiōng (chuanxiong)
  • Two and a half qian of fresh nanzhi (nanjing ginseng)
  • Half a tael each of raw and fried licorice, totaling seven qian

Grind these thoroughly; each dose is taken with two qian of the mixture, one cup of water, two slices of ginger, and three leaves of mint, boiled slowly until reduced to seven portions, and taken warm at any time.[55p]

Bai Xiang Pill: Treats children's cough with greenish vomiting.

Use red sprout cocklebur in appropriate amounts, dry it in the shade, boil with water until soft, remove the bones, expose it to sunlight until dry, then boil again with juice. Once the juice is completely evaporated, grind it into powder. Make small pills the size of millet, taking 10 to 20 pills each time and wash down with sesame soup, used as needed.

White Cake: Treats children's cough with phlegm and saliva from milk food.

Use talc, lightly powdered, wash with Ban Xia decoction, and roast. Each of Nán Xīng and Ba Dou, one qian (approximately 3 grams), prepare as powder. Take 24 pieces of Ba Dou, remove skin and membrane, boil with one liter of water until reduced. Grind the mixture well, mix with other medicines, and form into small pills the size of mung beans; form cakes. For children four years and older, take three to five cakes; for those under two years, take one to two cakes, and use green onion white soup before sleeping.

Small Chai Hu Decoction: Treats liver fire attacking the lungs, causing severe cough pain, possibly coarse breathing and heat symptoms.

Ingredients: Ren Shen (2 qian), Gan Cao (slightly roasted, 2 qian), Mai Men Dong (pits removed, 2 qian), Long Dan Cao (stir-fried in wine until black, 1 qian), Fang Feng (1 qian), Chai Hu (5 fen). Each time take 1 qian, decoct in water.

Huang Qin Ban Xia Sheng Jiang Decoction: Treats bile duct cough, with bitter vomiting resembling bile.

Ingredients: Huang Qin (1 qian), Sheng Jiang (1 qian), Gan Cao (roasted, 6 fen), Shao Yao (6 fen), Da Zao (2 pieces), Ban Xia (1 qian and 5 fen). Decoct and consume.[56p]

Peony and Licorice Decoction: Treats cough from the small intestine, with coughing accompanied by gas. Ingredients: one penny each of peony and roasted licorice. Decoction and take with water.

Black Plum Pill: Treats cough from the stomach accompanied by vomiting; if vomiting is severe, long worms may emerge. Ingredients: thirty black plums, six pennies each of asarum, prepared aconite, cassia twig, ginseng, and yellow bile; one tael each of dried ginger and coptis; four taels each of angelica and Sichuan pepper. Crush all ingredients into powder, soak the black plums in wine overnight, remove the pits, steam, and mix with mashed rice to make pills the size of tung seeds. Take ten pills with warm water.

Elevated Hemp Decoction: Treats cough from the spleen, with pain under the right rib that radiates to the shoulder and back; severe cases may not allow movement, and moving causes coughing of phlegm. Ingredients: equal parts of licorice, white peony, elevated hemp, and dried kudzu. Crush into powder, take one penny each time, decoction with water.

Red Stone Fat and Remaining Grain Decoction: Treats cough from the large intestine with fecal incontinence. Ingredients: two taels each of red stone fat and remaining grain, crushed together. Take two pennies each time, decoction with water.

Ephedra and Aconite with Asarum Decoction: Treats cough from the kidneys, with pain in the lower back that radiates when soft, severe cases lead to coughing of phlegm. Also treats cold evils attacking the teeth, leading to pain in the brain teeth; should be used urgently, as delays may lead to lack of salvation. Ingredients: two pennies each of ephedra and asarum; one penny of aconite.[57p]

Poria and Licorice Decoction treats bladder cough with urinary incontinence in cough. Poria two qian, cinnamon twig two and a half qian, five large slices of fresh ginger. Take two qian each time, decoct in water.

Xie Qing Pills treat facial redness from drinking, body heat with excessive phlegm, thick and sticky mucus, sore throat, wheezing, facial swelling, and vomiting food. Angelica, Sichuan lovage, and gentian root each one qian, rhubarb five fen, notopterygium, and gardenia fruit in equal parts. Grind into powder, form into honey pills the size of fox nuts. Take one pill, wash down with syrup. One formula adds licorice and peony.

Atractylodes Powder treats children’s cough with loss of internal fluids. One liang of atractylodes, lightly roasted, with each half liang of angelica, knotweed, lightly roasted, wood fragrance, and red peony, and honeyed licorice. Grind the medicine, sift roughly into powder. Take one qian each time, decoct in one small cup of water until reduced to five fen, strain, and adjust dosage according to child’s size without worrying about timing.

Wu Yao Decoction treats children’s red face and red lips, coarse breathing with fever, and cough with phlegm sounds. Use ma huang without removing the root nodes, apricot kernels without removing the skin tip, schizonepeta without removing the stems, and honey-water cooked and stir-fried platycodon, each five qian, with two and a half qian of licorice. Take two qian each time, with one cup of water, decoct until reduced to seven fen, and take warm without regard to time.[58p]

Qianghuo Powder treats the same condition as above.
Ingredients: Ginseng (remove the skin), Qianghuo, Red Poria (remove the skin), Chaihu (remove the skin), Xuanfu (remove the skin), Chuanxiong, Duhuo, Jiegang (cut and roast), Zhike, Cangzhu (process as previously), Licorice, each one tael. Grind together, take two qian per dose, with one cup of water, two slices of ginger, three leaves of mint, and boil down to seven parts. Take warm at any time. Qingmuxiang Decoction treats the same condition as above.
Ingredients: Qingmuxiang, Zhike (soaked, remove the chaff and roast), each half a tael; Licorice two and a half qian. Use this blend, take two qian per dose, with one cup of water, boil down to seven parts, and take warm at any time.

Fuling Houpo Decoction treats children with pale lips and faces, cough, excessive sweating on the forehead, long exhalations, reduced milk intake, and vomiting.
Ingredients: White Poria and Banxia (boil and roast), each seven and a half qian; roasted Licorice three qian; Houpo five qian (remove the coarse skin and crush). For each kilogram of this mix, use one pound of fresh ginger cut into thin slices, pound and mix well, soak overnight, and dry by slow fire. Use this mixture, take two qian per dose, with one and a half cups of water, three slices of ginger, and boil down to seven parts. Take warm at any time. Optionally, add one jujube (remove the core) and simmer together.[59p]

Huo Xiang Decoction - Treats the same condition.
Ren Shen (Ginseng) and Ban Xia (Pinellia) as before, Chi Fu Ling (Red Poria) and Zhi Gan Cao (Honey-fried Licorice) each one tael, Cang Zhu (Atractylodes) soaked in rice water overnight and filtered, then sliced and stir-fried until slightly yellow, two taels; Chen Pi (Dried Tangerine Peel) and Huo Xiang each seven qian and five fen; Hou Po (Magnolia Bark) prepared, one tael and five fen.

Take this mixture, chew; each dose two qian, with one bowl of water, two slices of ginger, and one date, decoct until seven parts remain, taken warm on an empty stomach. Alternatively, add roasted salt and decoct together.

Li Zhong Decoction - Treats the same condition.
Ren Shen (Ginseng) and Bai Zhu (Atractylodes) each one tael, Gan Jiang (Dried Ginger) and Zhi Gan Cao (Honey-fried Licorice) each two qian and five fen.

Grind the above into a powder; each dose half qian or one qian, with warm plain water, taken on an empty stomach. Alternatively, add Xing Ren (Apricot Kernel) and Bei Wu Wei Zi (Schizandra) to decoct together.

Xing Pi San - Treats cough due to Spleen deficiency.
Bai Zhu (Atractylodes) roasted with wall earth, Ren Shen (Ginseng), Gan Cao (Licorice), Ji Hong (Tangerine Peel), Bai Fu Ling (White Poria), and Quan Xie (Scorpion) each half tael; Ban Xia (Pinellia) and Mu Xiang (Aucklandia) each one fen; Bai Fu (White Aconite) four pieces; Nan Xing (Nasty Star) two pieces, the above two ingredients each processed; Chen Cang rice two hundred grains.

Grind the above into a powder; each dose one qian, with half a bowl of water, two slices of ginger, and half a date, decoct until two parts remain, taken gradually. In another method, without Bai Zhu and Ban Xia, adding one qian of lotus meat is also acceptable.[60p]

　　白附饮　治小儿风痰壅甚，肝木克制脾土，咳嗽过甚，顿作呕吐，乳食与痰俱出，方得少定。　　白附子　生南星　生半夏　生川乌去皮脐　明天麻　陈皮　南木香　全蝎去尾尖毒　僵蚕去丝　丁香各二钱　　右件銼，每服二钱，水一盏半，姜三片，慢火煎七分，作五次空心温服。
　　三拗汤　治感冒风邪，鼻塞声重，语音不出，或伤风冷，头疼目眩，四肢拘紧，咳嗽多痰，胸满气短。　　麻黄不去节　杏仁不去皮尖　甘草生用　　右各等分銼散，每服三钱，水一盏，生姜三片，煎至六分，去滓温服，取汗为度。一方，加荆芥、桔梗。嗽甚，加五味子，细辛各减半。又方，麻黄去节，杏仁去皮尖，甘草炙，名三和汤，治欬嗽尤妙。加减在乎活法。有热加前胡，伤风加荆芥，有痰加半夏。[61p]

Baifuzi Decoction treats severe wind-phlegm obstruction in children, where the wood element (liver) overcomes the earth element (spleen), leading to excessive coughing followed by vomiting, expelling both milk and phlegm, providing some relief.

Ingredients:

  • Baifuzi
  • Sheng Nanzhu
  • Sheng Banxia
  • Sheng Chuanwu (peeled and cored)
  • Ming Tianma
  • Chenpi
  • Nanmuxiang
  • Quanxie (tail and poisonous tip removed)
  • Jiangcan (silkworm, silk removed)
  • Dingxiang, each two qian.

Prepare by grinding the above, take two qian per dose, with one and a half cups of water, three slices of ginger, simmer over low heat for seven minutes, and take warm on an empty stomach five times.

Sanyao Decoction treats common cold with wind evil, nasal congestion with a heavy voice, inability to speak, or cold from wind causing headache and dizziness, stiffness in limbs, excessive coughing with phlegm, fullness in the chest, and shortness of breath.

Ingredients:

  • Mahuang (without joints)
  • Xingren (almonds without skins and tips)
  • Gancao (fresh)

Prepare by grinding the above in equal parts, take three qian per dose, with one cup of water and three slices of fresh ginger, simmer until reduced to six portions, strain and take warm, aiming to induce sweating.

An alternative includes adding Jingjie and Jiegeng. If cough is severe, add Wuweizi and Xixin, each reduced by half. Another formula substitutes Mahuang (without joints), Xingren (without skins and tips), and fried Gancao, named Sanhe Decoction, particularly effective for cough. Adjustments depend on individual treatments: add before Hu for heat, Jingjie for wind, and Banxia for phlegm.[61p]

Jia Jian San Yao Decoction
Ma Huang without roots and joints, three qian, boiled in water to remove foam, then dried. Gui Zhi two qian. Seven Xiong Ren, peeled and fried until yellow, then ground into a paste. Zhi Gan Cao one qian. Combine the above into a coarse powder, mix with almond paste evenly. Take one qian each time, with six fen of water, decoct until reduced to four fen, strain and take warm, at any time, based on sweating output, adjust dosage accordingly. If experiencing spontaneous sweating, it is not suitable for consumption.

Jin Fei Cao Powder
Treats wind injury with phlegm, dizziness and pain in the head, stiffness in the neck, alternating chills and fever, body aches, fullness in the chest, difficulty with phlegm and saliva, cough and wheezing, thick and sticky snot; also treats seasonal cold and epidemics with strong fever and aversion to wind.
Jing Jie four liang, Qian Hu three liang, Ma Huang without joints three liang, Xuan Fu Hua three liang, Zhi Gan Cao, Ban Xia soaked in ginger juice after washing seven times, Chi Shao each one liang.
Grind into powder, take two qian each time with one cup of water, three slices of fresh ginger, one jujube, decoct together until reduced to six fen, strain, and take at any time. If there is cold evil, then induce sweating. If coughing is severe, add Xiong Ren and Wu Wei Zi.[62p]

　　麦煎散 【《薛氏医案》，下同】 　治小儿夹惊伤寒，吐逆壮热，表里不解，气粗喘急，面赤自汗，或狂语惊叫，或不语无汗；及瘾疹遍身赤痒，往来潮热，时行麻痘疹子，余毒未尽，浑身浮肿，痰涎咳嗽；或变慢惊风，手足搐搦，眼目上视，及伤风头疼，并治之。　　滑石　地骨皮　赤芍　石膏　白茯苓　杏仁　葶苈子炒　人参各半两　麻黄去节，一两半　　右为末，每服一钱，麦子煎汤调下，如初生牙儿，感冒风冷，鼻寒身热，喷嚏多啼，每一字，用麦子煎汤调下。一方，去地骨皮、滑石，加羌活、川芎，薄荷煎汤调下。[63p]

Wheat Decoction Powder

This is used to treat children suffering from mixed colds, signs of shock, vomiting, intense heat, unrelieved exterior and interior symptoms, coarse breathing, flushed faces with spontaneous sweating, possible delirium, or silence with no sweating; also for widespread rash with itching, intermittent fevers, and symptoms of variola, residual toxins remaining, generalized edema, and cough with phlegm; or in cases of gradual seizures, convulsions in hands and feet, eyes looking upward, as well as for headaches caused by wind.

Ingredients:

  • Talc
  • Earth SKU (Dibone)
  • Red Peony
  • Gypsum
  • White Poria
  • Apricot Kernel
  • Stir-fried Lepidium
  • Ginseng, 7.5 grams each
  • Ephedra (remove the joints), 45 grams

Grind these into a powder, and for each dose, take 3 grams mixed with a decoction of wheat. This is suitable for infants with cold symptoms, having a cold body with a hot head, frequent sneezing and crying. Each dose should be administered in the wheat decoction.

Additionally, for another method, remove the Earth SKU and talc, and add Qianghuo and Chuanxiong, incorporating mint in the decoction for administration.[63p]

　　小青龙汤　治伤寒表不解，恶寒体热，水停心下，干呕发热而嗽，或渴或利，小便不利，或噎，小腹满喘。　　麻黄　赤芍　半夏炮　细辛　干姜炮　肉桂　甘草各七钱半　五味子半两　　右銼散，每服三钱，水一盏，煎七分，去滓加减服。微和者，去麻黄，加荛花如弹子大，炒令赤色。若噎者，去麻黄，加附子半钱炮。若小便不利者，加茯苓一两。若喘者，加杏仁去皮尖。若渴者，去半夏加(艹舌 )蒌根。[64p]

Xiao Qing Long Decoction is used to treat unrelieved exterior symptoms of excessive cold, with chills and fever, water retention under the heart, dry heaving, fever accompanied by cough, potential thirst or diarrhea, difficulty urinating, possible choking, and fullness in the lower abdomen with shortness of breath.

Ingredients:

  • Ephedra 7.5 grams
  • Red Peony Root 7.5 grams
  • Processed Pinellia 7.5 grams
  • Asarum 7.5 grams
  • Processed Dried Ginger 7.5 grams
  • Cinnamon 7.5 grams
  • Licorice 7.5 grams
  • Schisandra 15 grams

Grind the above into powder. Take 9 grams per dose, with one cup of water, simmer down to 70% and strain, adjusting as needed. For mild conditions, omit Ephedra and add flowering dogwood about the size of a ball, stir-fry until red. If there is choking, omit Ephedra and add 1.5 grams of processed Aconite. If there is difficulty urinating, add 30 grams of Poria. If there is shortness of breath, add blanched apricot kernels. If there is thirst, omit Pinellia and add the root of Trichosanthes.[64p]

　　人参荆芥散洁古方　治身热痰嗽，胸膈不利，宜下痰去热。　　人参半两　荆芥穗一两　大黄二钱
　　右为细末，水煎，调槟榔、木香细末五分，轻粉一字，乳后服。如身热潮热，宜服清凉饮子，去大黄；三服之后，一二日，却入大黄服之，令疏利则愈，不可便动脏腑。
　　解表散 【《证治准绳》，下同】 　主伤风感冷，咳嗽痰喘，呕吐泻利，惊悸有热，证在表里，并宜可投。　　麻黄制　杏仁汤泡去皮尖　赤茯苓各一两　川芎　防风　枳壳去穰，麸炒微黄，各一两半　甘草半生半炙，七钱五分　　右銼，每二钱，水一盏，姜二片，葱白一茎，煎七分，温服无时。有热，入薄荷同煎。[65p]

Ren Shen Jing Jie San is a classic remedy used to treat body heat, phlegm cough, and obstruction in the chest, suitable for clearing phlegm and removing heat.

The ingredients are:

  • 0.25 taels of ginseng
  • 1 tael of schizonepeta flower
  • 2 qians of rhubarb

Grind the above ingredients into a fine powder, then decoct with water. Add 0.5 qian each of betel nut and aromatic wood powder, and a pinch of light powder; take after meals. If there is body heat and fever, it is advisable to use a cooling drink and omit the rhubarb. After three doses, wait one or two days before reintroducing rhubarb to promote thorough elimination for recovery. Be careful not to disturb the internal organs too hastily.

Jie Biao San (Release the Exterior Powder) is indicated for symptoms of wind-cold, cough with phlegm and wheezing, vomiting, diarrhea, palpitations with heat, and conditions manifesting both externally and internally.

The ingredients are:

  • Ma Huang (Ephedra)
  • Almonds (peeled and soaked)
  • 1 tael each of crimson poria and Chuanxiong (Szechuan lovage)
  • 0.75 tael each of Fang Feng (Siler) and Zhi Qiao (bitter orange) (cooked until lightly yellow)
  • 0.375 taels of licorice (half raw and half roasted)

Grind the above and use 2 qians at a time, boil with a cup of water, 2 slices of ginger, and one stalk of scallion, simmer until reduced to 70%, and take warm at any time. If there’s heat, add mint and decoct together.[65p]

　　和解汤　治小儿感冒寒邪，壮热烦躁，鼻塞多涕，惊悸自汗，肢体疼痛，及疮疹已发未发，皆可服。　　羌活　防风　人参　川芎各一两　干葛　升麻　甘草　芍药各半两　　右銼散，每服三钱，姜枣煎服。一方加荆芥。无汗加麻黄。欬嗽者，加杏仁、五味子、桔梗。

Harmonizing Decoction treats children with colds caused by cold pathogens, causing strong heat and restlessness, nasal congestion with copious discharge, fright, spontaneous sweating, body aches, and rashes that may or may not have appeared. It can be taken by all.

Ingredients: Qianghuo, Fangfeng, Renshen, and Chuanxiong, each 1 tael; dried kudzu, Shengma, Gancao, and Shaoyao, each 0.5 tael.

Crush and mix the above, take 3 qian each time, decoct with ginger and jujube. For additional formula, add Jinge. If there is no sweating, add Mahuang. For coughing, add Xingren, Wuweizi, and Jiegeng.

Tianmendong Powder treats children with chest discomfort and cough due to heat.

Ingredients: Tianmendong (without heart-roasting), white mulberry root, red poria, Chaihu, lily, and Ziwun washed to remove soil, blue leaves, roasted licorice, each 0.5 tael.

Crush and sift the ingredients into powder, take 1 qian each time, boil with a small cup of water and a little fresh ginger until reduced by half, strain, and adjust the dose based on the child's size, taking warm.

Baibu Powder treats children with cough and heat, recommended for nursing mothers.

Ingredients: Baibu, slightly yellowed fritillary, Ziwun washed, kudzu root, each 1 tael; gypsum, 2 taels.

Crush and sift these into powder, take 3 qian each time, boil with a small cup of water and 2-7 pieces of bamboo leaves until reduced to 6 parts, strain, and take after meals. It is very beneficial for the infant to drink milk afterwards.[66p]

Huangqin Powder
For treating cough in children. Use Huangqin in whatever amount, soak it in a child's urine for three days, then take it out, grind it to powder, and dry it. The powder is to be taken in small amounts, either one or half a qian, mixed with a little warm water, and taken after meals.

Chaihu Shigao Decoction
For treating seasonal epidemics with severe heat, aversion to wind, headache, body aches, nasal congestion, chest fullness and discomfort, alternating chills and fever, cough, and thick phlegm.
Use 3.5 qian of mulberry root white skin and Huangqin, 2.5 qian of Cimicifuga, 5 qian each of gypsum, Chuanxiong, red peony, dried kudzu, and Chaihu, and 3 qian of Schizonepeta spikes. Grind these into a fine powder; each dose is 1 to 2 qian, with 2 slices of ginger and 10 grains of fermented soybeans, boiled in water.

Yangfei Decoction
Wash and dry 1 liang of purple aster, and wash 1 liang of Pinellia seven times. Use 1 liang of winter cress flower and true E-jiao (donkey-hide gelatin), and 0.5 liang each of ginseng and cinnamon heart. Grind these into a fine powder; each dose is 1 qian, with a small cup of water, add 2 slices of ginger and 5 grains of glutinous rice, boil until reduced to 1/5, strain, and take warm as needed.

Acorus Decoction
For treating lung wind evil, wheezing, and shoulder discomfort.
Use 1.9 inches of Acorus calamus, 1 liang of winter cress flower, wash and dry purple aster, and 1 liang each of ginseng and cinnamon heart. Grind these into a fine powder, mix with honey, pound in a stone mortar for 100-200 times until it becomes dough-like, and take 1 pill each time dissolved in boiled glutinous rice drink.[67p]

　　顺肺汤　治心肺不利，咳嗽。

　　陈橘皮散 【《圣惠方》】 　治小儿咳嗽，胸中满闷，不欲乳食。　　陈橘皮汤浸去白焙干　桔梗去芦　鸡苏　杏仁汤浸去皮尖，麸炒微黄　人参去芦，各一两　贝母煨微黄，半两　　右件捣罗为粗散，每服一钱，以水一小盏，入灯心十茎，煎至五分，去滓温服，日三四服，量儿大小。以意加减。[68p]

Wood Fragrance and Pinellia Treats Cold Stomach and Cough.
Wash wood fragrance and pinellia in water seven times, then dry. Take one tael each of dried nutmeg, patchouli leaves, cloves, and white atractylodes, and half a tael each of the above materials, finely powdered. Mix with fresh ginger juice to form pills the size of millet grains. Take ten pills each time, boiled in ginseng decoction, adjusting the dosage for children’s size.

Regulating Lung Decoction Treats Heart and Lung Insufficiency and Cough.
Wash perilla leaves and pinellia in water seven times, then dry, each one tael. Add five-flavor fruit, coltsfoot flowers, and Chen orange peel soaked in decoction, as well as half a tael each of cinnamon, wood fragrance. Grind into fine powder. Take one qian (a measurement) with eight parts water, adding small amounts of fresh ginger and ginseng, decoct until reduced to four parts, strain and take warm.

Chen Orange Peel Powder treats Children's Cough, Chest Congestion, and Loss of Appetite.
Soak dried Chen orange peel in water, then dry; wash the roots of platycodon; soak chicken perilla, and remove the skin from almonds. Lightly fry wheat bran until slightly yellow and prepare ginseng with the layers removed, each one tael. Lightly fry half a tael of fritillaria until slightly yellow. Grind them into coarse powder. Take one qian with a small cup of water, add ten strands of lampwick, boil until reduced to five parts, strain and take warm, three to four times a day, adjusting the dosage based on the child's size as needed.[68p]

　　麦门冬煎 【《证治准绳》，下同】 　治小儿咳嗽壮热，胸膈壅滞。　　麦门冬一两　生姜半两取汁　酥　蜜各二合　杏仁汤浸去皮尖双仁，一两　　右件药，先以水一大盏，煎麦门冬及杏仁至四分，入砂盆内研，绞取汁，却入银器中，次内生姜汁，慢火熬成，收于瓷器中，每服以清粥饮调下半茶匙，日三服，夜一服，量儿大小以意加减。

Maidong Decoction
Treats cough in children with strong heat and chest obstruction.
1 ounce Maidong, 0.5 ounce fresh ginger juice, 2 servings each of honey and clarified butter, 1 ounce peeled apricot kernels soaked in sweet almond soup.
First, boil Maidong and apricot kernels in 1 large cup of water until reduced to one-fourth. Grind in a mortar, strain to extract juice, then place into silverware. Next, add the ginger juice and simmer on low heat until thick, storing in porcelain. Each dose is mixed with half a teaspoon and taken with clear porridge, three times a day and once at night, adjusting dosage according to the child's size.

Mr. Mao's Milk Bean Paste
1/2 cup of chuan guo (fruit of Trichosanthes) and honey, 0.5 ounce of ginseng and lead white powder, 1/10 ounce of dried locust flower, and 120 chuan guo seeds.
First, combine chuan guo and honey to make a paste. Add all the powdered ingredients and mix into a paste. Each dose is the size of a large soybean, taken with apricot kernel decoction.

Lip Balm
Treats various coughs in children.
Three large pieces of curcuma, grated and soaked in ginger juice overnight; seven straight white silkworms; 0.5 cash of lead white powder, ground; one character worth of brain powder.
Grind these into fine powder, then mix with honey to form a paste. Apply a bean-sized amount to the child's lips — the size of a tung oil seed for children aged two to three, and the size of a soap piece for those ten and older, dissolved in mint and ginger soup.[69p]

Zihuan Powder: This treats children's cough.

Ginseng and Pinellia Pill (from "Standards of Diagnosis and Treatment")
Reduces phlegm and stops coughing.
Ginseng and Pinellia decoction washed seven times and roasted until dry, each one tael;
White Atractylodes, Sichuan ginger, and Tian Nansheng lightly toasted, each one tael.
Crush these into a powder, take fresh ginger juice, mix the powder into a dough consistency about the size of millet, take ten grains each time, and consume with ginger decoction. For infants under a month old, take a grain the size of a needle and dip it on the nipple for the child to suck.

Fritillaria Decoction
Treats lung stroke, cough, and wheezing fullness.
Fritillaria roasted until yellow, Pinellia and white alum decoction washed seven times and roasted until dry, each one tael;
Dried ginger, ephedra (roots removed), winter flower, and licorice, each half tael.
Crush these into a fine powder, take one qian each time, mix with a small cup of water, add three slices of fresh ginger and two almonds (skin removed), and cook until reduced by a fifth, then strain and take warm.

Astragalus Decoction from Ancient Texts
Treats children with cough, wheezing, body heat, and dry nose, indicating heat entering the lung channel.
Astragalus two taels, ginseng and licorice each two and a half qian, earth bone peel five qian, mulberry white peel three qian.
Crush these, boil in water and let cool, and take frequently.[72p]

　　加味四君子汤海藏方　治涎嗽。
　　人参　白朮土炒　白茯苓　甘草　杏仁　桑白皮各等分　半夏曲减半　　右，水煎服。又治咳嗽，用四君子末，煎紫苏汤调下。
　　细辛五味子汤 【《证治准绳》，下同】 　治肺经不足，胃气怯弱，或冒风邪，或停寒有饮，咳嗽倚息，不得安卧，胸　　满短气，干呕作热嗽，吐结痰，或吐涎沫，头目昏晕，身体疼重，语声不出，痛引胸胁，不问新久，并宜服之。　　细辛　半夏汤泡，各一两　罂粟壳去蒂盖炒　五味子各三两　乌梅去核　炙甘草各一两半　桑白皮炒，六钱　　右銼散，每服二钱，水一盏，生姜五片，煎至六分，去滓温服。

　　贝母汤　主百日内婴孩，咳嗽有痰。　　贝母一两　甘草半炙半生，二钱[73p]

Jiawei Sijunzi Decoction (Haicang Formula) for treating sputum cough.
Equal parts of: ginseng, white atractylodes (dry-fried), white poria, licorice, apricot kernel, mulberry root bark. Half the amount of pinellia. Decoct in water for ingestion. For cough, use powdered Sijunzi, decoct with perilla soup to take.

Xixin Wuweizi Decoction (from "Zhengzhi Zhuansheng") for treating lung meridian deficiency, weak stomach qi, potential exposure to wind pathogens, or stagnant cold with fluid retention, cough that worsens with reliance, difficulty in lying down comfortably, fullness in the chest with shortness of breath, dry retching causing heat cough, expectoration of phlegm or spittle, dizziness in the head, heaviness in the body, difficulty in speaking, pain radiating to the chest and ribs—suitable to take regardless of duration.
Ingredients: one tael each of xixin and pinellia, three taels of fried fruit of schisandra, one and a half taels of roasted licorice (pits removed), half tael of fried mulberry root bark. Prepare as a powder; take two qian each time, with one cup of water and five slices of fresh ginger, decoct to six parts, filter and take warm.

Baizhu Wuwei Decoction for treating cough with reversed qi and dyspnea.
Half tael each of: schisandra, white atractylodes, clove, ginseng, and coltsfoot flower; one qian of xixin (removing the soil). Grind into fine powder; take one qian each time, with eight parts water and three slices of ginger, decoct to four parts, filter, and take warm throughout the day.

Baimu Decoction for infants under a hundred days with cough and phlegm.
One tael of fritillaria; half tael of licorice, half roasted and half raw, two qian.[73p]

　　右件銼焙为末，每服一字或半钱，用陈米煎汤，空心调服；痰盛，淡姜汤调下。
　　比金圆 【《奇效良方》】 　治百晬内嗽，气粗痰盛，口疮眼热，发散后用之。　　人参　白茯苓　远志去心　山药　辰砂　明天麻　石菖蒲　川芎　炙甘草各一分　天南星炮，二钱，生姜汁制　麝香一字　　右为细末，炼蜜为丸皂子大，每服一粒，煎薄荷汤下。
